NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING 
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES 
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER 
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By  Order)
Commissioner  of  Stationery  and  Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
 
N. Vinothkumar, a Male child son of Thiru. K. Narayanan, born on 6th June 1990 residing at No.1, Ammamandapam
Road,  Srirangam, Tiruchirappalli-620 006 has been living  as Female. I have been granted Identity Card No.3214/2009 issued by
Tamil Nadu Gender Welfare Board, Social Welfare and NMP Department,  By this, I may be treated as Female and shall 
henceforth be known as SANTHIYA
Tiruchirappalli, 
N. VINOTHKUMAR
21st December 2020.
